
## Documentation Update - 2026-02-28 18:36
- ✅ Feature documentation generated: `docs/features/adult-player-phase9-compliance.md`
- Phase complete: Adult Player Lifecycle — Phase 9: Compliance Sprint (Adult Erasure, Data Retention & WCAG AA)

## PRD Audit - US-P9-008 - 2026-02-28 18:33:43
**PARTIAL** — US-P9-008 is substantially implemented with one minor gap.

## What's Implemented

**Emoji Rating Scale** — Full ARIA compliance in `apps/web/src/app/orgs/[orgId]/player/health-check/page.tsx`:
- `role="radiogroup"` + `aria-labelledby` on wrapper div (L768)
- Each button has `role="radio"`, `aria-checked`, and correct `aria-label` (e.g., "Very Poor — 1 out of 5") (L803)
- `<span className="sr-only">` inside each button (L837)
- `onKeyDown` handler for ArrowRight/Left/Up/Down navigation (L771-794)

**Focus Indicators** — `focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-blue-500 focus-visible:ring-offset-2` applied to emoji buttons; `FocusRing`/`FocusableItem` components in `src/components/accessibility/focus-visible.tsx`

**Org Theme Contrast Safeguard** — `getContrastColor()` in `src/lib/color-utils.ts` uses WCAG luminance threshold (0.179 = ~4.5:1 ratio); applied via `--org-primary-contrast` CSS variables in `use-org-theme.ts`

**Prefers-Reduced-Motion** — Global rule in `src/index.css` (L216-236) disables all `animate-*` classes and sets `transition-duration: 0.01ms` for all elements

## What's Missing

**Screen Reader Landmarks — Mobile sidebar lacks `<nav>`:** In `app-shell.tsx`, the desktop sidebar uses `<aside>` (not `<nav>`), and the mobile Sheet-based sidebar has no explicit `<nav>` or `role="navigation"`. The acceptance criteria requires `<nav>` or `role="navigation"` on the sidebar. This is a minor but clear gap.

---

The emoji scale, focus indicators, contrast safeguards, and reduced-motion are all fully implemented. Only the mobile navigation landmark is missing explicit `<nav>` semantics.

## PRD Audit - US-P9-UAT - 2026-02-28 18:42:41
**FAIL**

The story has significant gaps across most acceptance criteria.

**Critical issues:**

1. **Wrong filename** — File created as `compliance-phase9.spec.ts`, not `compliance.spec.ts` as specified.

2. **Erasure submission flow not tested** — Tests P9-004/005 verify button state but never actually submit the form. No test verifies the success toast or the transition to a Pending status card with deadline date.

3. **Second erasure request blocking not tested** — P9-003 only checks form OR status card exists; it doesn't verify the form is hidden when a pending request is active.

4. **Admin processing flow missing** — P9-008 only verifies the drawer opens. No test completes all category decisions, fills the response note, clicks "Process request", confirms the dialog, and verifies redirect + "Completed" status.

5. **Cross-role E2E missing** — No test verifies the player sees "Completed" status + admin response note after admin processes the request.

6. **Retention persistence not tested** — P9-013 only checks the save button is visible. No test sets a value, saves, reloads, and verifies persistence.

7. **Injury validation error not tested** — P9-012 checks the input is disabled/locked but doesn't attempt to set a value below 2555 and verify an error message.

8. **UAT report not updated** — `ralph-adult-player-phase9-compliance-US-P9-UAT-uat.md` shows "Pending Execution" with all checkboxes unchecked. The AC requires "All UI tests pass. Manual tests documented as passed."

**What passes:** Accessibility spec exists, manual test protocols are documented (not executed), and basic page/section visibility checks work.

# QA Verification Report — Phase 9: Compliance Sprint
**QA Agent** | **Date:** 2026-02-28 | **Overall:** PARTIAL PASS

## Summary Table

| Story | Status | Key Issues |
|-------|--------|-----------|
| US-P9-001 | PASS (warnings) | No admin auth on updateErasureRequestStatus; cross-org listPending |
| US-P9-002 | FAIL | executeApprovedErasureCategories is public not internal; COMMUNICATION_DATA uses hard-delete |
| US-P9-003 | PASS | Player UI fully implemented |
| US-P9-004 | PASS (warnings) | N+1 usePlayerName per row; no admin auth check |
| US-P9-005 | PARTIAL | No years unit selector; upcoming deletions only shows wellness count |
| US-P9-006 | WARN | Weekly digest logs only; no in-app notification; undefined index hack |
| US-P9-007 | PASS | axe-playwright correctly installed and configured |
| US-P9-008 | PASS | Emoji ARIA, focus indicators, prefers-reduced-motion all implemented |
| US-P9-009 | FAIL | Skip link targets div not main; no id=main-content in org layouts |
| US-P9-010 | PASS (warnings) | No admin role check on logBreach/updateBreachStatus |
| US-P9-UAT | FAIL | 2 test assertions use wrong text strings and will fail |

**TypeScript:** `npm run check-types` PASS (no new errors)

---

## CRITICAL Issues (Must Fix)

### CRITICAL-1: executeApprovedErasureCategories is PUBLIC, not internalAction
**File:** `packages/backend/convex/actions/retentionEnforcement.ts:20`
```typescript
export const executeApprovedErasureCategories = action({  // WRONG — must be internalAction
```
Any authenticated user can trigger irreversible data erasure on any player in any org. The PRD specifies this as an internal action. The admin UI calling it via `useAction(api.actions.retentionEnforcement.executeApprovedErasureCategories)` also breaks because `useAction` cannot call internal functions — the fix is: make it `internalAction`, add a thin public mutation wrapper that verifies admin role and calls `ctx.scheduler.runAfter(0, internal.actions.retentionEnforcement.executeApprovedErasureCategories, args)`.

### CRITICAL-2: No admin role authorization on updateErasureRequestStatus
**File:** `packages/backend/convex/models/erasureRequests.ts:268`
The mutation fetches the request and patches it with no role check. Any authenticated user with a valid `requestId` can change status to 'completed' or 'rejected' for any player's erasure request.

### CRITICAL-3: COMMUNICATION_DATA erasure uses ctx.db.delete() instead of soft-delete
**File:** `packages/backend/convex/models/retentionConfig.ts:293`
`softDeleteAllWellnessSessionsForPlayer` calls `ctx.db.delete(session._id)` directly, bypassing the 30-day grace period the PRD requires for all erasure execution paths. Change to `ctx.db.patch(session._id, { retentionExpired: true, retentionExpiredAt: Date.now() })` (requires adding these fields to the `whatsappWellnessSessions` schema).

### CRITICAL-4: Skip link targets non-focusable div; org layouts lack id="main-content"
**File:** `apps/web/src/app/layout.tsx:76`
Root layout: `<div id="main-content">` — must be `<main id="main-content" tabIndex={-1}>`.
**Files:** `apps/web/src/app/orgs/[orgId]/player/layout.tsx`, `admin/layout.tsx`
These layouts have `<main>` elements WITHOUT `id="main-content"`. The skip link in the root layout will jump to the outer wrapper div, not the page content. Each org-level layout needs `id="main-content"` on its `<main>` element (only one per page, the inner one should win).

### CRITICAL-5: Two E2E test assertions will fail at runtime
**File:** `apps/web/uat/tests/compliance-phase9.spec.ts`
- Line 82: `page.getByText("portability")` — UI shows "Rectification" (correct per PRD). Fix: check for "rectification" or "correct".
- Line 291: `page.getByRole("button", { name: /log breach/i })` — button says "Log new incident". Fix: change to `/log new incident/i`.

---

## Warnings (Should Fix)

**WARN-1** `packages/backend/convex/models/erasureRequests.ts:149`
`listPendingErasureRequests` filters by `organizationId` in memory after fetching all orgs' pending requests. The `by_deadline` index is `[status, deadline]` with no org scoping. Needs a `by_org_status_deadline [organizationId, status, deadline]` index or restructured query.

**WARN-2** `packages/backend/convex/models/retentionConfig.ts:138`, `breachRegister.ts:103,141`
`upsertOrgRetentionConfig`, `logBreach`, `updateBreachStatus` — all accept `organizationId` as an arg but do not verify the caller is an admin of that org.

**WARN-3** `packages/backend/convex/jobs/retentionEnforcement.ts:49`
```typescript
.withIndex("by_retention_expired", (q) => q.eq("retentionExpired", undefined as unknown as boolean))
```
This type-cast hack to query for undefined values in an index is unreliable in Convex and may not return expected results. The actual filtering relies on the subsequent `.filter(!r.retentionExpired)` call.

**WARN-4** `packages/backend/convex/jobs/retentionEnforcement.ts:332`
Weekly retention digest does NOT send in-app notifications to org admins as required by PRD. Only logs to console. Code comment acknowledges this as "future enhancement" but no tracking exists.

**WARN-5** `apps/web/src/app/orgs/[orgId]/admin/data-rights/page.tsx:163`
N+1 query pattern: `usePlayerName()` calls `getPlayerById` per row inside a `.map()`. Batch-fetch player identities instead.

**WARN-6** `packages/backend/convex/actions/retentionEnforcement.ts:1`
`"use node"` directive is unnecessary overhead. PRD explicitly says not required.

**WARN-7** `apps/web/src/app/orgs/[orgId]/admin/data-retention/page.tsx`
Input only accepts days. PRD requires days OR years unit selector.

## What Works Well (Evidence)

- **Schema** — All 4 new tables (`erasureRequests`, `orgRetentionConfig`, `retentionCronLogs`, `breachRegister`) correctly defined with all fields and indexes in `packages/backend/convex/schema.ts:5817-5913`
- **Erasure category map** — All 8 categories correct at `packages/backend/convex/lib/erasureCategoryMap.ts`
- **Player UI** — `data-rights-section.tsx` fully implements all PRD requirements: collapsible form, checkbox gating, status display, deadline warning, category outcomes
- **Admin review UI** — `admin/data-rights/page.tsx` implements per-category decision table with locked/unlocked logic, confirm dialog, overdue banner
- **Cron registration** — Both `enforceRetentionPolicy` (02:00 UTC) and `sendWeeklyRetentionDigest` (Monday 08:00 UTC) correctly registered in `crons.ts`
- **Navigation** — All 3 compliance pages (data-rights, data-retention, breach-register) linked in admin sidebar under 'Compliance' group
- **WCAG emoji scale** — Full ARIA implementation at `health-check/page.tsx:767-837` (radiogroup, role=radio, aria-checked, aria-label, sr-only text, arrow key navigation)

- **RetentionExpiresAt stamping** — Correctly stamped at `submitDailyHealthCheck` insertion using org config at `models/playerHealthChecks.ts:392-398`

## Code Review Gate - 2026-02-28 19:43:13

🔍 **Deep Code Review:** **VERDICT: BLOCK**

---

**ISSUES:**

- **[CRITICAL]** `breachRegister.ts:87-93` — `getBreachById` has **no auth check**. Any unauthenticated caller can fetch any breach record by ID. Needs `authComponent.safeGetAuthUser` guard.

- **[CRITICAL]** `erasureRequests.ts:158-164` — `getErasureRequestById` has **no auth check**. Exposes sensitive GDPR erasure data to unauthenticated users.

- **[CRITICAL]** `breachRegister.ts:159-175` — `updateBreachStatus` never verifies `breach.organizationId === args.organizationId`. An admin of org A can modify breach records belonging to org B by supplying org B's `breachId` with org A's `organizationId` (they pass the role check but mutate a different org's record).

- **[CRITICAL]** `erasureRequests.ts:291-308` — Same cross-org isolation gap in `updateErasureRequestStatus`: `ctx.db.get(args.requestId)` is patched without checking `request.organizationId === args.organizationId`.

- **[HIGH]** `erasureRequests.ts:269-308` — `updateErasureRequestStatus` accepts `adminUserId` as a **client-supplied argument**. A malicious admin can impersonate any userId. Should be derived server-side via `requireAuthAndOrg` (which already runs) — use the returned `userId` instead.

- **[HIGH]** `actions/retentionEnforcement.ts:61-73` — **N+1 query** inside the `for (const category of args.approvedCategories)` loop: `getErasureRequestByIdInternal` is called once per category. Fetch once before the loop, then reference the cached result.

- **[HIGH]** `jobs/retentionEnforcement.ts:45` — `softDeleteExpiredWellnessRecords` does a **full table scan** (`ctx.db.query("dailyPlayerHealthChecks").collect()`) with no index. Comment acknowledges this but it will hit Convex document limits in production. A `by_retentionExpiresAt` index is needed.

- **[HIGH]** `jobs/retentionEnforcement.ts:163-184` — `enforceRetentionPolicy` Phase 1 repeats the same full-table-scan pattern inline, compounding the issue.

- **[HIGH]** `jobs/retentionEnforcement.ts:125-127` — `q.gte("playerIdentityId", "" as never)` is a type-cast hack to force a full table scan. This bypasses type safety and is fragile. Same pattern at line 235.

- **[MEDIUM]** `actions/retentionEnforcement.ts:114,123,131` — `console.warn` in an action that runs in response to admin UI actions. Use structured error handling or rethrow instead of swallowing with a warn.

- **[MEDIUM]** `data-rights/page.tsx:151` (breach-register page.tsx:151) — `session?.user?.id` used for the auth check on the frontend. In Better Auth client sessions this is `id` not `_id`, so this is correct, but worth noting the asymmetry vs. backend `user._id`.

---

**Summary of must-fix before merge:**
1. Add auth guards to `getBreachById` and `getErasureRequestById`
2. Add cross-org ownership verification in `updateBreachStatus` and `updateErasureRequestStatus`
3. Remove `adminUserId` from client args in `updateErasureRequestStatus` — derive from session
4. Fix N+1 in `executeApprovedErasureCategories` action
5. Full table scans in retention jobs need an index before this hits production scale
